function mob_companion:update(delta)
  if xr_logic.try_switch_to_another_section(self.object, self.st, db.actor) then
    return
  end
  
  if not xr_logic.mob_captured(self.object) then
    self:reset_scheme()
    return
  end
  self:mob_move_to_actor()
end
